## Election

country_event = {
	id = germany_events.6

	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_events.6 option 1"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = GER_path option = DEFAULT } }
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = GER_path option = GER_PATH_SCHLEICHER_AUTDEM } }
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = GER_path option = GER_PATH_SCHLEICHER_PATAUT } }
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = GER_path option = GER_PATH_SOCLIB } }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_ai = yes }
			set_country_flag = GER_schleicher_ai
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_events.6 option 2"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = GER_path option = DEFAULT } }
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = GER_path option = GER_PATH_SWR_PATAUT } }
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = GER_path option = GER_PATH_SWR_AUTDEM } }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_ai = yes }
			set_country_flag = GER_swr_ai
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_events.6 option 3"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = GER_path option = DEFAULT } }
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = GER_path option = GER_PATH_SOCDEM } }
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = GER_path option = GER_PATH_SOCCON } }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_ai = yes }
			set_country_flag = GER_du_ai
		}
	}

	after = {
		country_event = { id = germany_events.7 days = 3 }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = germany_events.7
	title = germany_events.7.t
	desc = germany_events.7.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_cons #NEEDPIC

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_events.7 option germany_events.7.a"
		name = germany_events.7.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = GER_swr_ai
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = GER_playing_as_spd
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_playing_as_spd_tt
		set_variable = { GER_available_actions = 3 }
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = germany_events.13 days = 60 }
			country_event = { id = germany_events.61 days = 45 random_days = 45 }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = THIS decision = GER_SPD_consolidate_saxon_strongholds }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = THIS decision = GER_SPD_draft_popular_front_candidates }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = THIS decision = GER_SPD_left_liberal_cooperation }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = THIS decision = GER_SPD_rural_joint_slate_candidates }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = THIS decision = GER_SPD_selective_zentrum_cooperation }
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_events.7 option germany_events.7.b"
		name = germany_events.7.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = GER_du_ai
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = GER_playing_as_dvlp
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_playing_as_dvlp_tt
		set_variable = { GER_available_actions = 3 }
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = germany_events.14 days = 60 }
			country_event = { id = germany_events.17 days = 45 random_days = 45 }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = THIS decision = GER_DVLP_control_hesse }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = THIS decision = GER_DVLP_east_elbia_no_vote_split }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = THIS decision = GER_DVLP_westphalia_right_zentrum }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = THIS decision = GER_DVLP_national_liberal_seats }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = THIS decision = GER_DVLP_challenge_socialists_cities }
		}
	}
}

## Resignation of von Dirksen

country_event = {
	id = germany_events.8
	title = germany_events.8.t
	desc = germany_events.8.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_roedern

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_events.8 option germany_events.8.a"
		name = germany_events.8.a
		hidden_effect = {
			deactivate_advisor = GER_siegfried_von_roedern_advisor
			activate_advisor = GER_reichskanzler_in_prussia_advisor
		}
		activate_advisor = GER_siegfried_von_roedern_sic
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			long_name = GER_roedern_party_long
			name = GER_roedern_party
		}
		add_political_power = 50
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = GER_march_to_april
			add_idea = GER_march_to_april_2
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = germany_events.9 days = 7 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_events.8 option germany_events.8.b"
		name = germany_events.8.b
		hidden_effect = {
			deactivate_advisor = GER_siegfried_von_roedern_advisor
			activate_advisor = GER_reichskanzler_in_prussia_advisor
		}
		activate_advisor = GER_siegfried_von_roedern_sic
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			long_name = GER_roedern_party_long
			name = GER_roedern_party
		}
		add_political_power = 50
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_liberal }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = germany_events.10 days = 7 }
		}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = germany_events.9
	title = germany_events.9.t
	desc = germany_events.9.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_cons

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_events.9 option germany_events.9.a"
		name = germany_events.9.a
		add_political_power = -50
		add_stability = -0.1
		subtract_from_variable = { GER_LVP_seats = 4 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GER_liberal_seats > 0 }
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { GER_liberal_seats = 1 }
		}
		else = {
			subtract_from_variable = { GER_LVP_seats = 1 }
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = GER_SPD_seats
			value = 5
			tooltip = GER_SPD_gain
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { GER_DkP_seats = 1 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GER_agrarian_seats > 0 }
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { GER_agrarian_seats = 1 }
		}
		else = {
			subtract_from_variable = { GER_DkP_seats = 1 }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { GER_LVP_seats = 1 }
		add_to_variable = {
			var = GER_Zentrum_seats
			value = 3
			tooltip = GER_Zentrum_gain
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { GER_DkP_seats = 2 }
		add_to_variable = {
			var = GER_Guelph_seats
			value = 2
			tooltip = GER_Welfen_gain
		}

		end_coalition = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = end_coalition_tt
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = germany_events.10
	title = germany_events.10.t
	desc = germany_events.10.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_cons

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_events.10 option germany_events.10.a"
		name = germany_events.10.a
		add_political_power = -50
		add_stability = -0.1
		subtract_from_variable = { GER_SPD_seats = 2 }
		subtract_from_variable = { GER_LVP_seats = 2 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GER_agrarian_seats > 0 }
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { GER_agrarian_seats = 1 }
		}
		else = {
			subtract_from_variable = { GER_Zentrum_seats = 1 }
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = GER_DVLP_seats
			value = 5
			tooltip = GER_DVLP_gain
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { GER_SPD_seats = 1 }
		add_to_variable = { GER_farleft_seats = 1 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_farleft_1_gain
		subtract_from_variable = { GER_SPD_seats = 1 }
		add_to_variable = { GER_farright_seats = 1 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_farright_1_gain

		end_coalition = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = end_coalition_tt
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = germany_events.16
	title = germany_events.16.t
	desc = germany_events.16.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_cons

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_events.16 option germany_events.16.a"
		name = germany_events.16.a
		subtract_from_variable = { GER_SPD_seats = 1 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GER_farleft_seats > 0 }
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { GER_farleft_seats = 1 }
		}
		else = {
			subtract_from_variable = { GER_SPD_seats = 1 }
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = GER_Zentrum_seats
			value = 2
			tooltip = GER_Zentrum_gain
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { GER_LVP_seats = 1 }
		add_to_variable = { GER_Guelph_seats = 1 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_Welfen_1_gain
		subtract_from_variable = { GER_DkP_seats = 1 }
		add_to_variable = { GER_polish_seats = 1 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_Polish_1_gain
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_events.16 option germany_events.16.b"
		name = germany_events.16.b
		subtract_from_variable = { GER_DVLP_seats = 1 }
		subtract_from_variable = { GER_DkP_seats = 1 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GER_farright_seats > 0 }
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { GER_farright_seats = 1 }
		}
		else = {
			subtract_from_variable = { GER_DVLP_seats = 1 }
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = GER_Zentrum_seats
			value = 3
			tooltip = GER_Zentrum_gain
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GER_Guelph_seats > 4 }
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { GER_Guelph_seats = 5 }
			add_to_variable = { GER_Zentrum_seats = 1 }
			add_to_variable = { GER_LVP_seats = 4 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GER_Guelph_seats > 0 }
			}
			add_to_variable = { GER_Zentrum_seats = 1 }
			subtract_from_variable = { GER_Guelph_seats = 1 }
			add_to_variable = { GER_LVP_seats = GER_Guelph_seats }
			set_variable = { GER_Guelph_seats = 0 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_Welfen_collapse
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = germany_events.17
	title = germany_events.17.t
	desc = germany_events.17.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_cons #NEEDPIC

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_events.17 option germany_events.17.a"
		name = germany_events.17.a
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = national_populist
			popularity = 0.02
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { GER_SPD_seats = 3 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GER_liberal_seats > 0 }
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { GER_liberal_seats = 1 }
		}
		else = {
			subtract_from_variable = { GER_LVP_seats = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GER_farleft_seats > 0 }
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { GER_farleft_seats = 1 }
		}
		else = {
			subtract_from_variable = { GER_SPD_seats = 1 }
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = GER_DVLP_seats
			value = 5
			tooltip = GER_DVLP_gain
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GER_farleft_seats > 0 }
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { GER_farleft_seats = 1 }
		}
		else = {
			subtract_from_variable = { GER_SPD_seats = 1 }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { GER_SPD_seats = 1 }
		add_to_variable = {
			var = GER_farright_seats
			value = 2
			tooltip = GER_farright_gain
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { GER_SPD_seats = 1 }
		subtract_from_variable = { GER_LVP_seats = 1 }
		add_to_variable = {
			var = GER_liberal_seats
			value = 2
			tooltip = GER_liberal_gain
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_events.17 option germany_events.17.b"
		name = germany_events.17.b
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = national_populist
			popularity = 0.02
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { GER_Zentrum_seats = 3 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GER_polish_seats > 0 }
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { GER_polish_seats = 1 }
		}
		else = {
			subtract_from_variable = { GER_LVP_seats = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GER_Guelph_seats > 0 }
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { GER_Guelph_seats = 1 }
		}

		add_to_variable = {

			value = 5

		}

		if = {
			limit = {

			}
			subtract_from_variable = { GER_polish_seats = 1 }
		}

country_event = { # Papen joins with S-W-R (prevented by Zentrum Right or DVLP Ministries)
	id = germany_events.22
	title = germany_events.22.t
	desc = germany_events.22.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HOL_radio_red #NEEDPIC

	trigger = {
		GER_kurt_von_schleicher = { is_second_in_command = yes }
		NOT = { has_completed_focus = GER_zentrum_right }
		NOT = { has_completed_focus = GER_shuffle_prussian_ministries }
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_events.22 option germany_events.22.a"
		name = germany_events.22.a
		add_political_power = -10
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					is_in_array = { GER.swr_coalition_members_array = 10.id }
				}
			}
			add_to_array = { GER.swr_coalition_members_array = 10.id }
			add_to_variable = { GER_swr_coalition_seats = GER_Zentrum_seats_r }
			custom_effect_tooltip = GER_Zentrum_seats_r_join_swr
			subtract_from_variable = { GER_free_factions = 1 } # reduce number of free factions
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_array = { GER.democratic_union_members_array = 10.id }
			}
			remove_from_array = { GER.democratic_union_members_array = 10.id }
			subtract_from_variable = { GER_democratic_union_seats = GER_Zentrum_seats_r }
			custom_effect_tooltip = GER_Zentrum_seats_r_join_swr
			add_to_array = { GER.swr_coalition_members_array = 10.id }
			add_to_variable = { GER_swr_coalition_seats = GER_Zentrum_seats_r }
		}
		else = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
				popularity = 0.02
			}
		}
	}
}

	desc = germany_events.40.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_cons #NEEDPIC

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		GER_is_du_path = no
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = GER_anti_sedition_complete
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = GER_bauer_putsch
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			GER_democratic_resistance_event = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_events.40 option germany_events.40.a"
		name = germany_events.40.a
		add_political_power = -25
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_coalition_with_social_democrat = yes }
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				popularity = 0.02
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_democrat
				popularity = 0.01
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				popularity = 0.01
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Anti-Socialist Act
	id = germany_events.48
	title = germany_events.48.t
	desc = germany_events.48.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_cons #NEEDPIC

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		# Setup breakaway faction
		set_temp_variable = { temp1 = GER_DkP_seats }
		multiply_temp_variable = { temp1 = 0.1 }
		round_temp_variable = temp1
		set_temp_variable = { temp2 = GER_DkP_seats }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { temp2 = temp1 }
		set_variable = { GER_DkP_indy_seats = temp1 }
		set_variable = { GER_DkP_seats = temp2 }
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_events.48 option germany_events.48.a"
		name = germany_events.48.a
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			popularity = -0.05
		}
		# Remove them from the coalition
		subtract_from_variable = { GER_swr_coalition_number = GER_DkP_indy_seats }
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_DkP_indy_split_tt
		# If coalition number is now under 50%+1 of the Reichstag, start the failstate
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GER_swr_coalition_number < 223 }
			}
			country_event = germany_swr_events.32
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # THE WAR BEGINS
	id = germany_events.49
	title = germany_events.49.t
	desc = germany_events.49.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_cons #NEEDPIC

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_events.49 option germany_events.49.a"
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = GER_imperial_pride
			add_idea = GER_imperial_pride_2
		}
		name = germany_events.49.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_active_mission = GER_SPD_demand_action
			}
			remove_mission = GER_SPD_demand_action
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_active_mission = GER_coalition_relations
			}
			remove_mission = GER_coalition_relations
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_wartime_unpreparedness_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = germany_events.54 days = 7 }
			country_event = { id = germany_flavour_events.26 days = 365 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						GER_is_schleicher_path = yes
						GER_is_swr_path = yes
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = germany_flavour_events.95 days = 40 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GER_democratic_resistance_event_fired
				}
				country_event = { id = germany_events.52 days = 14 }
			}
			unlock_national_focus = GER_france_invaded
			set_variable = { GER_lacking_preparedness_modifier = -0.1 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { GER_debt > 150 }
					is_ai = no
				}
				add_to_variable = { GER_lacking_preparedness_modifier = -0.04 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { GER_debt > 180 }
					is_ai = no
				}
				add_to_variable = { GER_lacking_preparedness_modifier = -0.04 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { GER_debt > 199 }
					is_ai = no
				}
				add_to_variable = { GER_lacking_preparedness_modifier = -0.04 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						GER_carl_friedrich_goerdeler = { is_second_in_command = yes }
						GER_paul_lejeune_jung = { is_second_in_command = yes }
						GER_rudolf_schwander = { is_second_in_command = yes }
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = { GER_lacking_preparedness_modifier = -0.04 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_completed_focus = GER_nationalise_rail }
					NOT = { has_completed_focus = GER_railway_nationalisation }
					NOT = { has_completed_focus = GER_military_railways }
				}
				add_to_variable = { GER_lacking_preparedness_modifier = -0.02 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_completed_focus = GER_yearning_for_cannae
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = { GER_lacking_preparedness_modifier = -0.01 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_completed_focus = GER_einkreisung
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = { GER_lacking_preparedness_modifier = -0.01 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_completed_focus = GER_expand_kriegsschulen
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = { GER_lacking_preparedness_modifier = -0.01 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_completed_focus = GER_prepare_for_russia }
					NOT = { has_completed_focus = GER_prepare_for_france }
				}
				add_to_variable = { GER_lacking_preparedness_modifier = -0.01 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_completed_focus = GER_w_system
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = { GER_lacking_preparedness_modifier = -0.01 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_completed_focus = GER_industriewerke
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = { GER_lacking_preparedness_modifier = -0.01 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_completed_focus = GER_infantry_development }
					NOT = { has_completed_focus = GER_artillery_development }
					NOT = { has_completed_focus = GER_tank_development }
				}
				add_to_variable = { GER_lacking_preparedness_modifier = -0.01 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_completed_focus = GER_wever_doctrine }
					NOT = { has_completed_focus = GER_richthofen_doctrine }
					NOT = { has_completed_focus = GER_knauss_doctrine }
				}
				add_to_variable = { GER_lacking_preparedness_modifier = -0.02 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_completed_focus = GER_wegener_doctrine }
					NOT = { has_completed_focus = GER_raeder_doctrine }
				}
				add_to_variable = { GER_lacking_preparedness_modifier = -0.02 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { GER_completed_industrial_decisions < 10 }
				}
				add_to_variable = { GER_lacking_preparedness_modifier = -0.01 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { GER_completed_industrial_decisions < 5 }
				}
				add_to_variable = { GER_lacking_preparedness_modifier = -0.02 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = GER_national_defence_state
				}
				add_to_variable = { GER_lacking_preparedness_modifier = 0.02 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = GER_war_industry_nationalisation
				}
				add_to_variable = { GER_lacking_preparedness_modifier = 0.01 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = GER_no_idle_resources
				}
				add_to_variable = { GER_lacking_preparedness_modifier = 0.01 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = GER_mobilisation_protocols
				}
				add_to_variable = { GER_lacking_preparedness_modifier = 0.01 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = GER_society_control
				}
				add_to_variable = { GER_lacking_preparedness_modifier = 0.01 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = GER_propaganda_campaigns
				}
				add_to_variable = { GER_lacking_preparedness_modifier = 0.01 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GER_war_preparedness_act_passed
				}
				add_to_variable = { GER_lacking_preparedness_modifier = 0.02 }
			}
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GER_Lacking_Preparedness }
			set_variable = { GER_lacking_preparedness_modifier_2 = GER_lacking_preparedness_modifier }
			divide_variable = { GER_lacking_preparedness_modifier_2 = 2 }

			log = "KR_Event_Logging;GER Unpreparedness Modifier - [?GER.GER_lacking_preparedness_modifier]"

			# The modifier slowly removes, and you can make this process faster by taking focuses.
			country_event = { id = germany_events.50 days = 60 }
		}
	}
}
country_event = { # Reduction of the unpreparedness
	id = germany_events.50
	title = germany_events.50.t
	desc = germany_events.50.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_cons #NEEDPIC

	trigger = {
		has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GER_Lacking_Preparedness }
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_events.50 option germany_events.50.a"
		name = germany_events.50.a
		trigger = {
			has_war_with = FRA
			FRA = { has_capitulated = no }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { GER_lacking_preparedness_modifier < -0.02 } } }
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GER_Lacking_Preparedness }
			clear_variable = GER_lacking_preparedness_modifier
			clear_variable = GER_lacking_preparedness_modifier_2
		}
		else = {
			add_to_variable = { GER_lacking_preparedness_modifier = 0.02 }
			add_to_variable = { GER_lacking_preparedness_modifier_2 = 0.01 }
			force_update_dynamic_modifier = yes
			effect_tooltip = {
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = GER_unprepared_none
					add_idea = GER_unprepared_reduction
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { GER_completed_reduction_focuses < 1 }
					}
					country_event = { id = germany_events.50 days = 60 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { GER_completed_reduction_focuses < 2 }
					}
					country_event = { id = germany_events.50 days = 53 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { GER_completed_reduction_focuses < 3 }
					}
					country_event = { id = germany_events.50 days = 46 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { GER_completed_reduction_focuses < 4 }
					}
					country_event = { id = germany_events.50 days = 39 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { GER_completed_reduction_focuses < 5 }
					}
					country_event = { id = germany_events.50 days = 32 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { GER_completed_reduction_focuses < 6 }
					}
					country_event = { id = germany_events.50 days = 25 }
				}
				else = {
					country_event = { id = germany_events.50 days = 18 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_events.50 option germany_events.50.b"
		name = germany_events.50.b
		trigger = {
			FRA = {
				OR = {
					has_capitulated = yes
					exists = no
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { GER_lacking_preparedness_modifier < -0.02 } } }
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GER_Lacking_Preparedness }
			clear_variable = GER_lacking_preparedness_modifier
			clear_variable = GER_lacking_preparedness_modifier_2
		}
		else = {
			add_to_variable = { GER_lacking_preparedness_modifier = 0.02 }
			add_to_variable = { GER_lacking_preparedness_modifier_2 = 0.01 }
			force_update_dynamic_modifier = yes
			effect_tooltip = {
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = GER_unprepared_none
					add_idea = GER_unprepared_reduction
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { GER_completed_reduction_focuses < 1 }
					}
					country_event = { id = germany_events.50 days = 60 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { GER_completed_reduction_focuses < 2 }
					}
					country_event = { id = germany_events.50 days = 53 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { GER_completed_reduction_focuses < 3 }
					}
					country_event = { id = germany_events.50 days = 46 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { GER_completed_reduction_focuses < 4 }
					}
					country_event = { id = germany_events.50 days = 39 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { GER_completed_reduction_focuses < 5 }
					}
					country_event = { id = germany_events.50 days = 32 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { GER_completed_reduction_focuses < 6 }
					}
					country_event = { id = germany_events.50 days = 25 }
				}
				else = {
					country_event = { id = germany_events.50 days = 18 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_events.50 option germany_events.50.c"
		name = germany_events.50.c
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { GER_lacking_preparedness_modifier < -0.02 } } }
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GER_Lacking_Preparedness }
			clear_variable = GER_lacking_preparedness_modifier
			clear_variable = GER_lacking_preparedness_modifier_2
		}
		else = {
			add_to_variable = { GER_lacking_preparedness_modifier = 0.02 }
			add_to_variable = { GER_lacking_preparedness_modifier_2 = 0.01 }
			force_update_dynamic_modifier = yes
			effect_tooltip = {
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = GER_unprepared_none
					add_idea = GER_unprepared_reduction
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = GER_reduction_hidden_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { GER_completed_reduction_focuses < 1 }
					}
					country_event = { id = germany_events.51 days = 60 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { GER_completed_reduction_focuses < 2 }
					}
					country_event = { id = germany_events.51 days = 53 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { GER_completed_reduction_focuses < 3 }
					}
					country_event = { id = germany_events.51 days = 46 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { GER_completed_reduction_focuses < 4 }
					}
					country_event = { id = germany_events.51 days = 39 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { GER_completed_reduction_focuses < 5 }
					}
					country_event = { id = germany_events.51 days = 32 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { GER_completed_reduction_focuses < 6 }
					}
					country_event = { id = germany_events.51 days = 25 }
				}
				else = {
					country_event = { id = germany_events.51 days = 18 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
country_event = { # Reduction of the unpreparedness (hidden)
	id = germany_events.51

	trigger = {
		has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GER_Lacking_Preparedness }
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_events.51 option 1"
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { GER_lacking_preparedness_modifier < -0.02 } } }
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GER_Lacking_Preparedness }
			clear_variable = GER_lacking_preparedness_modifier
			clear_variable = GER_lacking_preparedness_modifier_2
		}
		else = {
			add_to_variable = { GER_lacking_preparedness_modifier = 0.02 }
			add_to_variable = { GER_lacking_preparedness_modifier_2 = 0.01 }
			force_update_dynamic_modifier = yes
			effect_tooltip = {
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = GER_unprepared_none
					add_idea = GER_unprepared_reduction
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { GER_completed_reduction_focuses < 1 }
					}
					country_event = { id = germany_events.51 days = 90 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { GER_completed_reduction_focuses < 2 }
					}
					country_event = { id = germany_events.51 days = 80 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { GER_completed_reduction_focuses < 3 }
					}
					country_event = { id = germany_events.51 days = 70 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { GER_completed_reduction_focuses < 4 }
					}
					country_event = { id = germany_events.51 days = 60 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { GER_completed_reduction_focuses < 5 }
					}
					country_event = { id = germany_events.51 days = 50 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { GER_completed_reduction_focuses < 6 }
					}
					country_event = { id = germany_events.51 days = 40 }
				}
				else = {
					country_event = { id = germany_events.51 days = 30 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

## Black Monday Setup

country_event = { #BM trigger event (MTTH to avoid the timeout bug, donotlog)
	id = germany_events.0
	hidden = yes

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		original_tag = GER
	}

	option = {
		set_temp_variable = { days_to_event = 34 }
		calculate_days_since_game_start = yes
		news_event = { id = germany_black_monday_events.0 days = days_to_event }
	}
}
news_event = {
	id = germany_black_monday_events.0
	immediate = { log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_black_monday_events.0" }
	title = germany_black_monday_events.0.t
	desc = germany_black_monday_events.0.d
	picture = GFX_news_event_GER_blackmonday1

	major = yes
	show_major = {
		NOT = {
			tag = GEA
			tag = MAF
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		GER = {
			hidden_effect = {
				add_named_threat = {
					threat = 4
					name = GER_black_monday_threat
				}
				add_stability = -0.40
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = GER_pre_black_monday
					add_idea = GER_black_monday_5
				}
				activate_mission = GER_black_monday_escalation
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			fire_black_monday_events = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = germany_black_monday_events.0.a
		trigger = {
			tag = GER
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_stability = -0.40
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = GER_pre_black_monday
				add_idea = GER_black_monday_5
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = crisis_in_progress

		subtract_from_variable = { GER_LVP_seats = 3 }
		subtract_from_variable = { GER_Zentrum_seats = 5 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GER_liberal_seats > 1 }
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { GER_liberal_seats = 2 }
		}
		else = {
			subtract_from_variable = { GER_LVP_seats = 2 }
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = GER_SPD_seats
			value = 10
			tooltip = GER_SPD_gain
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { GER_Zentrum_seats = 3 }
		subtract_from_variable = { GER_DkP_seats = 5 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GER_agrarian_seats > 1 }
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { GER_agrarian_seats = 2 }
		}
		else = {
			subtract_from_variable = { GER_Zentrum_seats = 2 }
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = GER_DVLP_seats
			value = 10
			tooltip = GER_DVLP_gain
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = germany_black_monday_events.0.b
		trigger = {
			has_socialist_government = no
			NOT = {
				tag = GER
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = germany_black_monday_events.0.c
		trigger = { has_socialist_government = yes }
	}

	after = {
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_named_threat = {
				threat = 4
				name = GER_black_monday_threat
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # IT'S TIME TO DUEL
	id = germany_black_monday_events.4
	title = germany_black_monday_events.4.t
	desc = germany_black_monday_events.4.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_reichstag2 #NEEDPIC

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_black_monday_events.4 option germany_black_monday_events.4.a"
		name = germany_black_monday_events.4.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = { rule = GER_card_game option = GER_CARD_GAME_DISABLED }
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_ideas = GER_black_monday_10
			}
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = GER_disabled_black_monday_10
				days = 180
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = GER_disabled_black_monday_tt
		}
		else = {
			set_country_flag = GER_black_monday_game_active
			set_variable = { GER_bm_game_rounds = 1 } # increments by 1 every turn. will be useful later
			set_variable = { GER_economic_health = -10 } # -10 - worst level. -1 - fixed economy.
			set_variable = { GER_economic_decline = 2500 } # Temp value. Will be replaced with some way to generate scaling up stats for the crisis.
			set_variable = { GER_stagnation = 2500 } # Temp value. Will be replaced with some way to generate scaling up stats for the crisis.
			set_variable = { GER_debt = 105 } # Starting debt value. >200 means default
			set_variable = { GER_crisis_id = 1 } # test
			#Variables needed to easily display economic health effects
			set_variable = { GER_consumer_goods_loss = 0.5 }
			set_variable = { GER_factory_output_loss = -0.4 }
			set_variable = { GER_building_production_loss = -0.4 }
			set_variable = { GER_max_efficiency_loss = -0.4 }
			GER_initialize_bm_game = yes
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Debt Default
	id = germany_black_monday_events.8
	title = germany_black_monday_events.8.t
	desc = germany_black_monday_events.8.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_Blackweekover

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_black_monday_events.8 option germany_black_monday_events.8.a"
		name = germany_black_monday_events.8.a
		add_stability = -0.5
		add_war_support = -0.5
		clr_country_flag = GER_black_monday_game_active
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_black_monday_game_over_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			GER_bm_game_end = yes # Effect which clears all the Black Monday card game stuff
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_ideas = GER_debt_default_1 # Reduced by 5% for 10 years, then converts Black Monday to a yearly reducible spirit.
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_debt_default_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = GER_debt_default_1
				days = 365
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = GER_ruhrkampf_begun
			}
			add_to_variable = { # Measures strength. Need to be 25-75 at the end of each Ruhrkampf turn
				var = GER_ruhrkampf_strength
				value = 40
				tooltip = GER_ruhrkampf_raised
			}
			clamp_variable = { var = GER_ruhrkampf_strength max = 100 min = 0 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				GER_is_du_path = yes
			}
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = GER_Z_loyalty
				value = 20
				tooltip = GER_Z_loyalty_loss
			}
			clamp_variable = { var = GER_Z_loyalty min = 0 max = 100 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { GER_Z_loyalty < 1 }
					is_in_coalition_with_social_conservative = yes
				}
				activate_mission = GER_SPD_Z_rift
			}
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = GER_LVP_loyalty
				value = 20
				tooltip = GER_LVP_loyalty_loss
			}
			clamp_variable = { var = GER_LVP_loyalty min = 0 max = 100 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { GER_LVP_loyalty < 1 }
					is_in_coalition_with_social_liberal = yes
				}
				activate_mission = GER_SPD_LVP_rift
			}
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = GER_Left_SPD_loyalty
				value = 20
				tooltip = GER_Left_SPD_loyalty_loss
			}
			clamp_variable = { var = GER_Left_SPD_loyalty min = 0 max = 100 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { GER_Left_SPD_loyalty < 1 }
					has_country_flag = GER_left_spd_in_coalition
				}
				activate_mission = GER_SPD_Left_rift
			}
		}
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				GER_is_in_mitteleuropa = yes
			}
			effect_tooltip = {
				add_ideas = GER_debt_default_6
			}
			country_event = germany_black_monday_events.9
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = germany_schleicher_events.1
	title = germany_schleicher_events.1.t
	desc = germany_schleicher_events.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_schleicher2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_completed_focus = GER_von_schleicher_cabinet }
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				long_name = GER_schleicher_party_long
				name = GER_schleicher_party
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_schleicher_events.1 option germany_schleicher_events.1.a"
		name = germany_schleicher_events.1.a
		add_stability = 0.02
		remove_ideas = GER_march_to_april
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_ideas = GER_march_to_april_2
			news_event = germany_flavour_events.35
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				popularity = -0.04
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
				popularity = 0.06
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_conservative
				long_name = GER_true_social_conservative_party_long
				name = GER_true_social_conservative_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
				long_name = GER_authoritarian_democrat_party_long
				name = GER_authoritarian_democrat_party
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
				election_frequency = 60
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
		}
		activate_advisor = GER_kurt_von_schleicher_sic
		effect_tooltip = {
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
				election_frequency = 60
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			complete_national_focus = GER_von_schleicher_cabinet
			deactivate_advisor = GER_reichskanzler_in_prussia_advisor
			activate_advisor = GER_siegfried_von_roedern_advisor
			country_event = { id = germany_schleicher_events.2 days = 3 }
			clr_country_flag = GER_playing_as_spd
			clr_country_flag = GER_playing_as_dvlp
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { GER_DkP_seats < 50 }
				}
				country_event = { id = germany_events.62 days = 200 }
			}
			set_variable = { GER_schleicher_ideology = 50 } # USED BY SCHLEICHER MECHANICS
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_kurt_von_schleicher_sic_tt
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = germany_schleicher_events.2
	title = germany_schleicher_events.2.t
	desc = germany_schleicher_events.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_schleicher3

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_schleicher_events.2 option germany_schleicher_events.2.a"
		name = germany_schleicher_events.2.a
		add_stability = 0.02
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		complete_national_focus = GER_arbeitsschlacht
		complete_national_focus = GER_constructive_no_confidence
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_schleicher_mechanics_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = GER_schleicher_mechanics_flag
			# Seat variables
			set_variable = { GER_farleft_seats_r = GER_farleft_seats } # id 1
			set_variable = { GER_SPD_seats_r = GER_SPD_seats } # id 2

			set_temp_variable = { temp1 = GER_LVP_seats } #Splits LVP into two factions
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = SPD_left_LVP_boosted
				}
				multiply_temp_variable = { temp1 = 0.65 }
				round_temp_variable = temp1
			}
			else = {
				multiply_temp_variable = { temp1 = 0.5 }
				round_temp_variable = temp1
			}
			set_temp_variable = { temp2 = GER_LVP_seats }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { temp2 = temp1 }
			set_variable = { GER_LVP_seats_l = temp1 } # id 3
			set_variable = { GER_LVP_seats_r = temp2 } # id 4
			set_variable = { GER_Guelph_seats_r = GER_Guelph_seats } # id 5
			set_variable = { GER_liberal_seats_r = GER_liberal_seats } # id 6
			set_variable = { GER_polish_seats_r = GER_polish_seats } # id 7
			set_temp_variable = { temp3 = GER_Zentrum_seats } #Splits Zentrum into three factions
			set_temp_variable = { temp4 = GER_Zentrum_seats }
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GER_left_zentrum_boosted
				}
				multiply_temp_variable = { temp3 = 0.4 }
				round_temp_variable = temp3
				multiply_temp_variable = { temp4 = 0.3 }
				round_temp_variable = temp4
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GER_right_zentrum_boosted
				}
				multiply_temp_variable = { temp3 = 0.3 }
				round_temp_variable = temp3
				multiply_temp_variable = { temp4 = 0.3 }
				round_temp_variable = temp4
			}
			else = {
				multiply_temp_variable = { temp3 = 0.3 }
				round_temp_variable = temp3
				multiply_temp_variable = { temp4 = 0.4 }
				round_temp_variable = temp4
			}
			set_temp_variable = { temp5 = GER_Zentrum_seats }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { temp5 = temp3 }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { temp5 = temp4 }
			set_variable = { GER_Zentrum_seats_l = temp3 } # id 8
			set_variable = { GER_Zentrum_seats_c = temp4 } # id 9
			set_variable = { GER_Zentrum_seats_r = temp5 } # id 10

			set_variable = { GER_agrarian_seats_r = GER_agrarian_seats } # id 11
			set_variable = { GER_DkP_seats_r = GER_DkP_seats } # id 12
			set_variable = { GER_DVLP_seats_r = GER_DVLP_seats } # id 13
			set_variable = { GER_farright_seats_r = GER_farright_seats } # id 14
			#Total seats - 445
			add_to_array = { GER.democratic_union_members_array = 1.id }
			add_to_array = { GER.democratic_union_members_array = 2.id }
			set_variable = { GER_democratic_union_seats = GER_farleft_seats_r }
			add_to_variable = { GER_democratic_union_seats = GER_SPD_seats_r }
			add_to_array = { GER.swr_coalition_members_array = 13.id }
			add_to_array = { GER.swr_coalition_members_array = 14.id }
			set_variable = { GER_swr_coalition_seats = GER_farright_seats_r }
			add_to_variable = { GER_swr_coalition_seats = GER_DVLP_seats_r }
			#set up faction protection decisions
			set_variable = { GER_max_faction_targets = 3 } # Is shown in tooltip, can be raised by focus
			set_variable = { GER_available_faction_targets = GER_max_faction_targets } # Refreshed with GER_max_faction_targets every turn

			activate_mission = GER_democratic_union_alignment_turn

			activate_targeted_decision = { target = 1 decision = GER_Defend_Reichstag_Faction }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = 2 decision = GER_Defend_Reichstag_Faction }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = 3 decision = GER_Defend_Reichstag_Faction }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = 4 decision = GER_Defend_Reichstag_Faction }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = 5 decision = GER_Defend_Reichstag_Faction }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = 6 decision = GER_Defend_Reichstag_Faction }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = 7 decision = GER_Defend_Reichstag_Faction }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = 8 decision = GER_Defend_Reichstag_Faction }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = 9 decision = GER_Defend_Reichstag_Faction }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = 10 decision = GER_Defend_Reichstag_Faction }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = 11 decision = GER_Defend_Reichstag_Faction }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = 12 decision = GER_Defend_Reichstag_Faction }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = 13 decision = GER_Defend_Reichstag_Faction }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = 14 decision = GER_Defend_Reichstag_Faction }

			activate_mission = GER_swr_alignment_turn

			# Set up an array of all state ids
			add_to_array = { GER.GER_factions_states = 1.id }
			add_to_array = { GER.GER_factions_states = 2.id }
			add_to_array = { GER.GER_factions_states = 3.id }
			add_to_array = { GER.GER_factions_states = 4.id }
			add_to_array = { GER.GER_factions_states = 5.id }
			add_to_array = { GER.GER_factions_states = 6.id }
			add_to_array = { GER.GER_factions_states = 7.id }
			add_to_array = { GER.GER_factions_states = 8.id }
			add_to_array = { GER.GER_factions_states = 9.id }
			add_to_array = { GER.GER_factions_states = 10.id }
			add_to_array = { GER.GER_factions_states = 11.id }
			add_to_array = { GER.GER_factions_states = 12.id }
			add_to_array = { GER.GER_factions_states = 13.id }
			add_to_array = { GER.GER_factions_states = 14.id }

			# Set up variable to check for how many factions are still free
			set_variable = { GER_free_factions = 10 }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = germany_schleicher_events.3 days = 3 }
			country_event = { id = germany_schleicher_events.4 days = 7 }
			country_event = { id = germany_schleicher_events.8 days = 50 random_days = 10 }
		}
	}
}

	desc = germany_schleicher_events.44.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_BEL_Protest_Aggressive

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_schleicher_events.44 option germany_schleicher_events.44.a"
		name = germany_schleicher_events.44.a
		subtract_from_variable = { # Measures strength. Need to be 25-75 at the end of each Ruhrkampf turn
			var = GER_ruhrkampf_strength
			value = 10
			tooltip = GER_ruhrkampf_reduced
		}
		clamp_variable = { var = GER_ruhrkampf_strength max = 100 min = 0 }
		add_stability = -0.2
		set_country_flag = GER_reichexec_unsuccessful # for the Schleicher mechanics
		59 = { #Hanover
			add_manpower = -500
			if = {
				limit = { has_resistance = yes }
				cancel_resistance = yes
			}
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GER_Brunswick }
			hidden_effect = {
				force_enable_resistance = { occupier = GER occupied = GRU clear = yes }
				remove_core_of = GRU
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			GRU = { drop_cosmetic_tag = yes }
			FRA = {
				country_event = { id = germany_flavour_events.119 days = 2 }
			}
			ENG = {
				country_event = { id = germany_flavour_events.119 days = 2 }
			}
		}
	}
}

### Schwarz-Weiss-Rot events

country_event = { # Setup
	id = germany_swr_events.1
	title = germany_swr_events.1.t
	desc = germany_swr_events.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_swr

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "KR_Event_Logging;GER Political Path - SWR"
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_swr_events.1 option germany_swr_events.1.a"
		name = germany_swr_events.1.a
		add_stability = 0.2
		every_character = {
			limit = {
				has_trait = KR_prussian_minister_president
				NOT = {
					is_character = GER_ewald_von_kleist_schmenzin
				}
			}
			retire = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			GER_ewald_von_kleist_schmenzin = {
				remove_political_advisor_role = yes
			}
		}
		set_variable = { GER_swr_coalition_balance = 50 } # 0 is full DkP, 100 is full DVLP
		set_variable = { GER_swr_foci_taken = 0 }
		hidden_effect = {
			GER_ulrich_von_hassell = { set_nationality = GER }
			activate_advisor = GER_ulrich_von_hassell_advisor
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = available_political_advisor
		show_ideas_tooltip = GER_ulrich_von_hassell_advisor
		custom_effect_tooltip = is_hired
		hidden_effect = {
			#AI picking
			country_event = germany_swr_events.100
			# Hugenberg Crisis
			country_event = { id = germany_swr_events.3 days = 11 }
			# Z events
			country_event = { id = germany_swr_events.4 days = 7 }
			country_event = { id = germany_swr_events.5 days = 7 }
			country_event = { id = germany_swr_events.6 days = 7 }
			# Agrarian Crisis
			country_event = { id = germany_swr_events.8 days = 120 }
			# Wilhelm II event
			country_event = { id = germany_flavour_events.92 days = 30 }
			# Reichsbanner event
			country_event = { id = germany_flavour_events.96 days = 365 }
			# New Police Union
			country_event = { id = germany_flavour_events.109 days = 180 }
		}
		# Set up coalition size
		set_variable = { GER_swr_coalition_number = GER_DVLP_seats }
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_array = { GER.swr_coalition_members_array = 14.id } #Far Right
			}
			add_to_variable = { GER_swr_coalition_number = GER_farright_seats }
		}
		#13 is DVLP, always in coalition
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_array = { GER.swr_coalition_members_array = 12.id } #DkP
			}
			add_to_variable = { GER_swr_coalition_number = GER_DkP_seats }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_array = { GER.swr_coalition_members_array = 11.id } #Agrarians
			}
			set_country_flag = GER_swr_agrarians_in_coalition
			add_to_variable = { GER_swr_coalition_number = GER_agrarian_seats }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_in_array = { GER.swr_coalition_members_array = 10.id } #Zentrum-R
					is_in_array = { GER.swr_coalition_members_array = 9.id } #Zentrum-C
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { GER_swr_coalition_number = GER_Zentrum_seats_r }
			add_to_variable = { GER_swr_coalition_number = GER_Zentrum_seats_c }
			set_variable = { GER_swr_zentrum_deputies = 0 }
			add_to_variable = { GER_swr_zentrum_deputies = GER_Zentrum_seats_r }
			add_to_variable = { GER_swr_zentrum_deputies = GER_Zentrum_seats_c }
			set_country_flag = GER_zentrum_swr_coalition
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_country_flag = GER_zentrum_right_chairman
							has_country_flag = GER_zentrum_centre_chairman
						}
					}
					country_event = { id = germany_flavour_events.99 days = 200 } # Zentrum event
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_array = { GER.swr_coalition_members_array = 9.id } #Zentrum-C needed to add Zentrum-L
			}
			add_to_variable = { GER_swr_coalition_number = GER_Zentrum_seats_l }
			add_to_variable = { GER_swr_zentrum_deputies = GER_Zentrum_seats_l }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_array = { GER.swr_coalition_members_array = 7.id } #Polish Party
			}
			add_to_variable = { GER_swr_coalition_number = GER_polish_seats_r }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_array = { GER.swr_coalition_members_array = 6.id } #Liberal Parties
			}
			add_to_variable = { GER_swr_coalition_number = GER_liberal_seats }
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:market_liberal }
			add_to_coalition = yes
			set_country_flag = GER_swr_natlibs_in_coalition
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_array = { GER.swr_coalition_members_array = 5.id } #Guelphs
			}
			add_to_variable = { GER_swr_coalition_number = GER_Guelph_seats }
			set_country_flag = GER_swr_guelphs_in_coalition
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = yes
				has_country_flag = GER_schleicher_ai
			}
			clr_country_flag = GER_schleicher_ai
			set_country_flag = GER_swr_ai
		}
	}
}
country_event = { # Hugenberg
	id = germany_swr_events.2
	title = germany_swr_events.2.t
	desc = germany_swr_events.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_hugenberg

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_swr_events.2 option germany_swr_events.2.a"
		name = germany_swr_events.2.a
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = national_populist
			popularity = 0.01
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_effect_increases_dvlp_tt
		add_to_variable = { GER_swr_coalition_balance = 10 }
		GER_check_swr_coalition_strength = yes
		# Set up number of DVLP deputies aligned with Hugenberg
		set_temp_variable = { temp1 = GER_DVLP_seats }
		multiply_temp_variable = { temp1 = 0.35 }
		round_temp_variable = temp1
		set_temp_variable = { temp2 = GER_DVLP_seats }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { temp2 = temp1 }
		set_variable = { GER_DVLP_seats_hug = temp1 }
		set_variable = { GER_DVLP_seats_has = temp2 }
		# Rift between Has and Hug. Percentage from 0-100
		set_variable = { GER_hugenberg_faction_rift = 25 }
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = germany_swr_events.16 days = 4 }
			country_event = { id = germany_swr_events.17 days = 60 random_days = 7 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_hugenberg_appointed_tt
		if = {
			limit = { is_ai = yes }
			set_country_flag = GER_hugenberg_ai #Activates AI Strategy
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = GER_zentrum_swr_coalition
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			custom_effect_tooltip = GER_zentrum_swr_coalition_hurts_tt
			add_to_variable = { GER_Zentrum_seats_r = -3 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_swr_events.2 option germany_swr_events.2.b"
		name = germany_swr_events.2.b
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		add_political_power = -25
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_hugenberg_not_appointed_tt

		# Set up number of DVLP deputies aligned with Hugenberg. This is separate from germany_swr_events.2.a because the starting percentage of seats is different
		set_temp_variable = { temp1 = GER_DVLP_seats }
		multiply_temp_variable = { temp1 = 0.3 }
		round_temp_variable = temp1
		set_temp_variable = { temp2 = GER_DVLP_seats }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { temp2 = temp1 }
		set_variable = { GER_DVLP_seats_hug = temp1 }
		set_variable = { GER_DVLP_seats_has = temp2 }
		# Rift between Has and Hug. Percentage from 0-100
		set_variable = { GER_hugenberg_faction_rift = 35 }
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = germany_swr_events.33 days = 60 random_days = 7 }
		}
	}
}

		round_temp_variable = GER_KVP_seats_temp
		set_temp_variable = { GER_DkP_seats_temp = GER_DkP_seats }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { GER_DkP_seats_temp = GER_KVP_seats_temp }
		set_variable = { GER_KVP_seats = GER_KVP_seats_temp }
		set_variable = { GER_DkP_seats = GER_DkP_seats_temp }
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_swr_events.27 option germany_swr_events.27.a"
		name = germany_swr_events.27.a
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = -0.1
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_effect_increases_dvlp_tt
		add_to_variable = { GER_swr_coalition_balance = 50 }
		GER_check_swr_coalition_strength = yes
		# Remove Volkskonservatives from the coalition
		subtract_from_variable = { GER_swr_coalition_number = GER_KVP_seats }
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_KVP_split_tt
		# If coalition number is now under 50%+1 of the Reichstag, start the failstate
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GER_swr_coalition_number < 223 }
			}
			country_event = germany_swr_events.32
		}
		else = {
			# Else Hugenberg challenges Hassell
			country_event = { id = germany_swr_events.28 days = 2 }
		}
	}
}

			remove_targeted_decision = { target = THIS decision = GER_hugenberg_welfare_strike }
			remove_targeted_decision = { target = THIS decision = GER_hugenberg_economic_deregulation }
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_swr_events.29 option germany_swr_events.29.a"

			clr_country_flag = GER_hugenberg_ai
		}
		clr_country_flag = GER_hugenberg_mechanics_begin
		add_stability = 0.1
		if = {
			limit = { is_ai = no }
			add_political_power = 50
		}
		else = { add_political_power = 200 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_effect_increases_dvlp_tt
		add_to_variable = { GER_swr_coalition_balance = 10 }

			remove_mission = GER_DVLP_schmidt_alignment
			remove_mission = GER_DVLP_levetzow_alignment
			remove_mission = GER_DVLP_trotha_alignment
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = GER_zentrum_swr_coalition
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			custom_effect_tooltip = GER_zentrum_swr_coalition_helps_tt

	}

		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_swr_events.30 option germany_swr_events.30.a"

			remove_mission = GER_DVLP_schmidt_alignment
			remove_mission = GER_DVLP_levetzow_alignment
			remove_mission = GER_DVLP_trotha_alignment

country_event = { # Coalition Collapses
	id = germany_swr_events.46
	title = germany_swr_events.46.t
	desc = germany_swr_events.46.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_cons # NEEDPIC

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "KR_Event_Logging;GER Political Path - Lejeune-Jung Cabinet"
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_swr_events.46 option germany_swr_events.46.a"
		name = germany_swr_events.46.a
		set_country_flag = GER_failed_swr_government
		hidden_effect = {
			GER_paul_lejeune_jung = {
				remove_political_advisor_role = yes
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { GER_is_in_mitteleuropa = yes }
				remove_ideas = GER_paul_lejeune_jung_effect
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
				long_name = GER_authoritarian_democrat_party_long
				name = GER_authoritarian_democrat_party
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				popularity = 0.1
			}
		}
		activate_advisor = GER_paul_lejeune_jung_sic
		GER_ulrich_von_hassell = {
			remove_political_advisor_role = yes
		}
		uncomplete_national_focus = {
			focus = GER_vanquish_parliamentarism
			uncomplete_children = yes
		}
		uncomplete_national_focus = {
			focus = GER_national_social_principle
			uncomplete_children = yes
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			long_name = GER_lejeune_party_long
			name = GER_lejeune_party
		}
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:paternal_autocrat }
		remove_from_coalition = yes
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_conservative }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { GER.coalition_stability = 0.50 }
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
				long_name = GER_paternal_autocrat_party_long
				name = GER_paternal_autocrat_party
			}
			remove_ideas = {
				GER_natpop_economics_1
				GER_natpop_economics_2
				GER_natpop_economics_12
				GER_corporate_state_idea_2
				GER_corporate_state_idea_1
			}
			GER_adolf_von_trotha = {
				remove_political_advisor_role = yes
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						region = 37 # Baltic States
						region = 38 # Poland
						state = 785 # Lorraine
						state = 948 # Liège
						AND = {
							state = 741 # Verviers
							NOT = { is_owned_by = ROOT }
						}
						AND = {
							state = 978 # Limburg
							NOT = { is_owned_by = ROOT }
						}
					}
				}
				remove_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Ambassador Crisis End
	id = germany_swr_events.64
	title = germany_swr_events.64.t
	desc = germany_swr_events.64.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_hassell2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		# Setup breakaway faction
		set_temp_variable = { temp1 = GER_DVLP_seats }
		multiply_temp_variable = { temp1 = 0.07 }
		round_temp_variable = temp1
		set_temp_variable = { temp2 = GER_DVLP_seats }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { temp2 = temp1 }
		set_variable = { GER_DVLP_indy_seats = temp1 }
		set_variable = { GER_DVLP_seats = temp2 }
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_swr_events.64 option germany_swr_events.64.a"
		name = germany_swr_events.64.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = GER
			}
			add_named_threat = {
				threat = -1
				name = ambassador_crisis_threat_end
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = GER_effect_increases_dkp_tt
			add_to_variable = { GER_swr_coalition_balance = -25 }
			GER_check_swr_coalition_strength = yes
			# Remove them from the coalition
			subtract_from_variable = { GER_swr_coalition_number = GER_DVLP_indy_seats }
			custom_effect_tooltip = GER_DVLP_indy_split_tt
			# If coalition number is now under 50%+1 of the Reichstag, start the failstate
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { GER_swr_coalition_number < 223 }
				}
				country_event = germany_swr_events.32
			}
		}
		else = {
			effect_tooltip = {
				add_named_threat = {
					threat = -1

country_event = { # Ambassador Crisis End
	id = germany_swr_events.66
	title = germany_swr_events.66.t
	desc = germany_swr_events.66.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_swr

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		# Setup breakaway faction
		set_temp_variable = { temp1 = GER_DVLP_seats }
		multiply_temp_variable = { temp1 = 0.07 }
		round_temp_variable = temp1
		set_temp_variable = { temp2 = GER_DVLP_seats }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { temp2 = temp1 }
		set_variable = { GER_DVLP_indy_seats = temp1 }
		set_variable = { GER_DVLP_seats = temp2 }
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_swr_events.66 option germany_swr_events.66.a"
		name = germany_swr_events.66.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = GER
			}
			add_named_threat = {
				threat = 4
				name = ambassador_crisis_threat_end
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = GER_effect_increases_dkp_tt
			add_to_variable = { GER_swr_coalition_balance = -25 }
			GER_check_swr_coalition_strength = yes
			# Remove them from the coalition
			subtract_from_variable = { GER_swr_coalition_number = GER_DVLP_indy_seats }
			custom_effect_tooltip = GER_DVLP_indy_split_tt
			# If coalition number is now under 50%+1 of the Reichstag, start the failstate
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { GER_swr_coalition_number < 223 }
				}
				country_event = germany_swr_events.32
			}
		}
		else = {
			effect_tooltip = {
				add_named_threat = {
					threat = 4
					name = ambassador_crisis_threat_end
				}
			}
		}
		add_war_support = 0.1
	}
}

country_event = { # Ambassador Crisis
	id = germany_swr_events.74
	title = germany_swr_events.74.t
	desc = germany_swr_events.74.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NOR_navy

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_swr_events.74 option germany_swr_events.74.a"
		name = germany_swr_events.74.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				OR = {
					has_global_flag = GER_ENG_escalate
					has_global_flag = GER_GER_escalate
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_depends_on_opponent_tt
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = ENG
			}
			set_global_flag = GER_ENG_escalate
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				tag = GER
			}
			set_global_flag = GER_GER_escalate
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_swr_events.74 option germany_swr_events.74.b"
		name = germany_swr_events.74.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				OR = {
					has_global_flag = GER_ENG_back_down
					has_global_flag = GER_GER_back_down
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_depends_on_opponent_tt
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = ENG
			}
			set_global_flag = GER_ENG_back_down
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				tag = GER
			}
			set_global_flag = GER_GER_back_down
		}
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_ai = no
					ENG = {
						is_ai = yes
					}
				}
				country_event = germany_swr_events.600 # set up the global flags and their results there
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					tag = GER
				}
				country_event = germany_swr_events.600 # set up the global flags and their results there
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # DkP chairman event
	id = germany_swr_events.96
	title = germany_swr_events.96.t
	desc = germany_swr_events.96.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_westarp

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_swr_events.96 option germany_swr_events.96.a"
		name = germany_swr_events.96.a
		trigger = {
			GER_is_swr_path = yes
			OR = {
				GER_ulrich_von_hassell = {
					has_trait = KR_leader_of_dvlp_average
				}
				NOT = {
					GER_ulrich_von_hassell = {
						has_advisor_role = political_advisor
					}
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_treviranus_wins_tt
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_effect_increases_dkp_tt
		add_to_variable = { GER_swr_coalition_balance = -15 }
		GER_check_swr_coalition_strength = yes
		set_country_flag = GER_treviranus_co_chair
		country_event = germany_swr_events.97
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_swr_events.96 option germany_swr_events.96.b"
		name = germany_swr_events.96.b
		trigger = {
			GER_is_swr_path = yes
			OR = {
				GER_ulrich_von_hassell = {
					has_trait = KR_leader_of_dvlp_average
				}
				NOT = {
					GER_ulrich_von_hassell = {
						has_advisor_role = political_advisor
					}
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_schlange_wins_tt
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_effect_increases_dvlp_tt
		add_to_variable = { GER_swr_coalition_balance = 15 }
		GER_check_swr_coalition_strength = yes
		set_country_flag = GER_schlange_co_chair
		country_event = germany_swr_events.98
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_swr_events.96 option germany_swr_events.96.c"
		name = germany_swr_events.96.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					GER_ulrich_von_hassell = {
						has_advisor_role = political_advisor
					}
					NOT = {
						GER_ulrich_von_hassell = {
							has_trait = KR_leader_of_dvlp_average
						}
					}
				}
				GER_is_schleicher_path = yes
				GER_is_du_path = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					GER_ulrich_von_hassell = {
						has_trait = KR_leader_of_dvlp_low
					}
					GER_ulrich_von_hassell = {
						has_trait = KR_leader_of_dvlp_min
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = {
							GER_ulrich_von_hassell = {
								has_advisor_role = political_advisor
							}
						}
						GER_is_swr_path = yes
					}
					GER_is_schleicher_path = yes
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = GER_treviranus_wins_tt
			if = {
				limit = {
					GER_is_swr_path = yes
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = GER_effect_increases_dkp_tt
				add_to_variable = { GER_swr_coalition_balance = -15 }
				GER_check_swr_coalition_strength = yes
			}
			set_country_flag = GER_treviranus_co_chair
		}
		else = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = GER_schlange_wins_tt
			if = {
				limit = {
					GER_is_swr_path = yes
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = GER_effect_increases_dvlp_tt
				add_to_variable = { GER_swr_coalition_balance = 15 }
				GER_check_swr_coalition_strength = yes
			}
			set_country_flag = GER_schlange_co_chair
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Zentrum splits
	id = germany_swr_events.102
	title = germany_swr_events.102.t
	desc = germany_swr_events.102.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_zentrumchange

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_swr_events.102 option germany_swr_events.102.a"
		name = germany_swr_events.102.a
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = -0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		# Remove non-Right Zentrum from the coalition
		subtract_from_variable = { GER_swr_coalition_number = GER_swr_zentrum_deputies }
		add_to_variable = { GER_swr_coalition_number = GER_Zentrum_seats_r }
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_Z_swr_split_tt
		set_country_flag = GER_federalist_union_established # for a post-DNVB event

		# If coalition number is now under 50%+1 of the Reichstag, start the failstate
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GER_swr_coalition_number < 223 }
			}
			country_event = germany_swr_events.32
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #LVP/NLP deputies join
	id = germany_swr_events.105
	title = germany_swr_events.105.t
	desc = germany_swr_events.105.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_rochus_rheinbaben

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	immediate = {
		set_variable = { GER_LVP_seats_to_NLP = GER_LVP_seats_r }
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_array = { GER.swr_coalition_members_array = 3.id } # has LVP left
			}
			divide_variable = { GER_LVP_seats_to_NLP = 2 }
		}
		else = {
			divide_variable = { GER_LVP_seats_to_NLP = 4 }
		}
		round_variable = GER_LVP_seats_to_NLP
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_swr_events.105 option germany_swr_events.105.a"
		name = germany_swr_events.105.a
		add_to_variable = { GER_swr_coalition_number = GER_LVP_seats_to_NLP }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GER_liberal_seats > 2 }
				NOT = {
					is_in_array = { GER.swr_coalition_members_array = 6.id } #doesn't have minor liberals
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { GER_swr_coalition_number = 2 }
			subtract_from_variable = { GER_liberal_seats = 2 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = germany_swr_events.105.tta
		}
		else = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = germany_swr_events.105.ttb
		}
	}
}

### Demokratische Union Events

country_event = { # Setup
	id = germany_spd_events.1
	title = germany_spd_events.1.t
	desc = germany_spd_events.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_cons # NEEDPIC

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		log = "KR_Event_Logging;GER Political Path - SPD"
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_spd_events.1 option germany_spd_events.1.a"
		name = germany_spd_events.1.a
		add_stability = 0.2
		every_character = {
			limit = {
				has_trait = KR_prussian_minister_president
				NOT = {
					is_character = GER_ewald_von_kleist_schmenzin
				}
			}
			retire = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			GER_ewald_von_kleist_schmenzin = {
				remove_political_advisor_role = yes
			}
		}
		# Set up coalition size
		set_variable = { GER_du_coalition_number = GER_SPD_seats }
		set_country_flag = GER_left_spd_in_coalition
		set_variable = { GER_Left_SPD_loyalty = 70 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp6 = GER_SPD_seats }
		multiply_temp_variable = { temp6 = 0.25 }
		set_variable = { GER_Left_SPD_seats = temp6 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_array = { GER.democratic_union_members_array = 3.id } # has at least LVP (Left)
			}
			add_to_variable = { GER_du_coalition_number = GER_LVP_seats }
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_liberal }
			add_to_coalition = yes
			set_variable = { GER_LVP_loyalty = 50 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = SPD_left_LVP_boosted
				}
				add_to_variable = { GER_LVP_loyalty = 10 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_in_array = { GER.democratic_union_members_array = 8.id } # has at least Zentrum (Left)
					has_country_flag = GER_spd_came_to_power_via_ruhrkampf
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { GER_du_coalition_number = GER_Zentrum_seats_l }
			add_to_variable = { GER_du_coalition_number = GER_Zentrum_seats_c }
			add_to_variable = { GER_Z_seats_in_coalition = GER_Zentrum_seats_l }
			add_to_variable = { GER_Z_seats_in_coalition = GER_Zentrum_seats_c }
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_conservative }
			add_to_coalition = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_array = { GER.democratic_union_members_array = 9.id } # has Zentrum (Centre)
				}
				add_to_variable = { GER_du_coalition_number = GER_Zentrum_seats_r }
				add_to_variable = { GER_Z_seats_in_coalition = GER_Zentrum_seats_r }
			}
			set_variable = { GER_Z_loyalty = 50 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GER_left_zentrum_boosted
				}
				add_to_variable = { GER_Z_loyalty = 5 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GER_right_zentrum_boosted
				}
				add_to_variable = { GER_Z_loyalty = -5 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GER_zentrum_left_chairman
				}
				add_to_variable = { GER_Z_loyalty = 10 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GER_zentrum_centre_chairman
				}
				add_to_variable = { GER_Z_loyalty = -5 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GER_zentrum_right_chairman
				}
				add_to_variable = { GER_Z_loyalty = -20 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_array = { GER.democratic_union_members_array = 7.id }
			}
			add_to_variable = { GER_du_coalition_number = GER_polish_seats }
			set_country_flag = GER_poles_in_coalition
			custom_effect_tooltip = POL_add_to_coalition
			set_variable = { GER_Polish_loyalty = 50 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GER_polish_list_not_happy_flag
				}
				add_to_variable = { GER_Polish_loyalty = -10 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_array = { GER.democratic_union_members_array = 11.id }
			}
			add_to_variable = { GER_du_coalition_number = GER_agrarian_seats }
			set_country_flag = GER_agrarians_in_coalition
			custom_effect_tooltip = agr_add_to_coalition
			set_variable = { GER_Agrarian_loyalty = 50 }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			activate_mission = GER_coalition_relations
		}
		country_event = germany_spd_events.2
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = yes
				has_country_flag = GER_schleicher_ai
			}
			clr_country_flag = GER_schleicher_ai
			set_country_flag = GER_du_ai
		}
	}
}

				value = 20
				tooltip = GER_LVP_loyalty_loss
			}

			}

		}

country_event = { # Mission: Crush Prussia
	id = germany_spd_events.15
	title = germany_spd_events.15.t
	desc = germany_spd_events.15.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_prussia

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_spd_events.15 option germany_spd_events.15.a"
		name = germany_spd_events.15.a
		add_ideas = GER_prussian_budget_crisis
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GER_Government_Paralysis }
			}
			effect_tooltip = {
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = GER_paralysis_reduce_5
					add_idea = GER_paralysis_base
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { GER_government_paralysis_factor = -0.05 }
			clamp_variable = {
				var = GER_government_paralysis_factor
				max = 0
				min = -1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = social_democrat
				OR = {
					AND = {
						is_ai = yes
						check_variable = { GER_government_paralysis_factor < -0.69 } # AI cheat
					}
					AND = {
						is_ai = no
						check_variable = { GER_government_paralysis_factor < -0.49 }
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = germany_spd_events.53
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = {
			localization_key = EFFECT_UNLOCK_DECISION_CATEGORY
			NAME = GER_prussian_budget_crisis
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { GER_prussia_victories = 0 } # Need at least 3 (of 4?) to claim victory.
			activate_mission = GER_SPD_prussian_budget_crisis_defeat
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = THIS decision = GER_SPD_prussia_mp_schleicher }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = THIS decision = GER_SPD_prussia_schleicher_negotiate }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = THIS decision = GER_SPD_prussia_agriculture_concessions }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = THIS decision = GER_SPD_prussia_national_liberals }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = THIS decision = GER_SPD_prussia_house_boycott }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = THIS decision = GER_SPD_prussia_adenauer_communication }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # New Prussia Election
	id = germany_spd_events.20
	title = germany_spd_events.20.t
	desc = germany_spd_events.20.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_mechanized_farms

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_spd_events.20 option germany_spd_events.20.a"
		name = germany_spd_events.20.a # A strong policy that strengthens SPD in particular, and weakens the Agrarians.
		ai_chance = { base = 50 }
		subtract_from_variable = { GER_Prussia_Agrarian_seats = 4 }
		subtract_from_variable = { GER_Prussia_DkP_seats = 6 }
		add_to_variable = { GER_Prussia_Left_seats = 10 }
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_spd_events.20 option germany_spd_events.20.b"
		name = germany_spd_events.20.b # Boosts the LVP somewhat, but is quite weak and actually strengthens DkP (junkers threatened by estate seizure)
		ai_chance = { base = 5 }
		subtract_from_variable = { GER_Prussia_Agrarian_seats = 2 }
		subtract_from_variable = { GER_Prussia_Right_seats = 4 }
		subtract_from_variable = { GER_Prussia_Left_seats = 1 }
		add_to_variable = { GER_Prussia_LVP_seats = 6 }
		subtract_from_variable = { GER_Prussia_NLP_seats = 1 }
		subtract_from_variable = { GER_Prussia_Left_seats = 1 }
		add_to_variable = { GER_Prussia_DkP_seats = 2 }
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_spd_events.20 option germany_spd_events.20.c"
		name = germany_spd_events.20.c # A very weak policy, since it offers no structural changes.
		ai_chance = { base = 5 }
		subtract_from_variable = { GER_Prussia_DkP_seats = 3 }
		add_to_variable = { GER_Prussia_Left_seats = 3 }
		subtract_from_variable = { GER_Prussia_NLP_seats = 2 }
		add_to_variable = { GER_Prussia_Zentrum_seats = 2 }
		subtract_from_variable = { GER_Prussia_NLP_seats = 2 }
		add_to_variable = { GER_Prussia_LVP_seats = 2 }
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = germany_spd_events.21 days = 3 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # New Prussia Election
	id = germany_spd_events.21
	title = germany_spd_events.21.t
	desc = germany_spd_events.21.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_POL_german_officer

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_spd_events.21 option germany_spd_events.21.a"
		name = germany_spd_events.21.a # This is really despised by people in East Elbia and mobilizes them, but Poles turn out as well.
		subtract_from_variable = { GER_Prussia_LVP_seats = 2 }
		subtract_from_variable = { GER_Prussia_Left_seats = 2 }
		add_to_variable = { GER_Prussia_DkP_seats = 4 }
		subtract_from_variable = { GER_Prussia_Left_seats = 2 }
		add_to_variable = { GER_Prussia_Right_seats = 2 }
		subtract_from_variable = { GER_Prussia_NLP_seats = 2 }
		subtract_from_variable = { GER_Prussia_Zentrum_seats = 1 }
		add_to_variable = { GER_Prussia_Polish_seats = 3 }
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_spd_events.21 option germany_spd_events.21.b"
		name = germany_spd_events.21.b # Makes Poles really hate you, and less of them turn out.
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = GER_poles_in_coalition
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { GER_Prussia_LVP_seats = 1 }
		add_to_variable = { GER_Prussia_DkP_seats = 1 }
		add_to_variable = { GER_Prussia_NLP_seats = 1 }
		subtract_from_variable = { GER_Prussia_Polish_seats = 3 }
		subtract_from_variable = {
			var = GER_Polish_loyalty
			value = 25
			tooltip = GER_Polish_loyalty_loss
		}
		clamp_variable = { var = GER_Polish_loyalty min = 0 max = 100 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GER_Polish_loyalty < 1 }
				has_country_flag = GER_poles_in_coalition
			}
			activate_mission = GER_SPD_Polish_rift
		}
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = germany_spd_events.22 days = 3 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # New Prussia Election
	id = germany_spd_events.22
	title = germany_spd_events.22.t
	desc = germany_spd_events.22.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_prussia

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_spd_events.22 option germany_spd_events.22.a"
		name = germany_spd_events.22.a # Unpopular policy, but it brings a few seats for SPD.
		subtract_from_variable = { GER_Prussia_Right_seats = 3 }
		add_to_variable = { GER_Prussia_Left_seats = 3 }
		subtract_from_variable = { GER_Prussia_LVP_seats = 3 }
		subtract_from_variable = { GER_Prussia_Zentrum_seats = 2 }
		add_to_variable = { GER_Prussia_DkP_seats = 5 }
		subtract_from_variable = { GER_Prussia_Zentrum_seats = 2 }
		add_to_variable = { GER_Prussia_NLP_seats = 2 }
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_spd_events.22 option germany_spd_events.22.b"
		name = germany_spd_events.22.b # Makes very little change.
		subtract_from_variable = { GER_Prussia_Right_seats = 3 }
		add_to_variable = { GER_Prussia_Left_seats = 3 }
		subtract_from_variable = { GER_Prussia_DkP_seats = 3 }
		add_to_variable = { GER_Prussia_LVP_seats = 3 }
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			# Results processing.
			set_variable = { GER_Prussia_coalition = GER_Prussia_Left_seats }
			if = {
				limit = { is_in_coalition_with_social_liberal = yes }
				add_to_variable = { GER_Prussia_coalition = GER_Prussia_LVP_seats }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_in_coalition_with_social_conservative = yes }
				add_to_variable = { GER_Prussia_coalition = GER_Prussia_Zentrum_seats }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = GER_poles_in_coalition }
				add_to_variable = { GER_Prussia_coalition = GER_Prussia_Polish_seats }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = GER_agrarians_in_coalition }
				add_to_variable = { GER_Prussia_coalition = GER_Prussia_Agrarian_seats }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = GER_Prussian_NLP_support }
				add_to_variable = { GER_Prussia_coalition = GER_Prussia_NLP_seats }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						check_variable = { GER_Prussia_coalition > 221 }
						is_ai = yes
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = germany_spd_events.23 days = 3 }
			}
			else = {
				country_event = { id = germany_spd_events.24 days = 3 }
			}
		}
	}
}
