					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = GER_schleicher_cooperative_prussia
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					add = -10
					has_country_flag = GER_zentrum_left_chairman
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = GER_schleicher_cooperative_prussia
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					add = -20
					has_country_flag = GER_schleicher_cooperative_prussia
				}
				country_event = germany_spd_events.36 # Failure
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_spd_events.34 option germany_spd_events.34.b"
		name = germany_spd_events.34.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				has_country_flag = GER_schleicher_cooperative_prussia
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = GER_zentrum_left_chairman
					has_country_flag = GER_zentrum_centre_chairman
				}
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			seed = global.date
			60 = {
				modifier = {
					add = -20
					is_in_coalition_with_social_conservative = no
				}
				modifier = {
					add = 10
					has_country_flag = GER_zentrum_centre_chairman
				}
				modifier = {
					add = 20
					has_country_flag = GER_zentrum_left_chairman
				}
				modifier = {
					add = 20
					has_country_flag = GER_schleicher_cooperative_prussia
				}
				country_event = germany_spd_events.35 # Success
			}
			40 = {
				modifier = {
					add = 20
					is_in_coalition_with_social_conservative = no
				}
				modifier = {
					add = -10
					has_country_flag = GER_zentrum_centre_chairman
				}
				modifier = {
					add = -20
					has_country_flag = GER_zentrum_left_chairman
				}
				modifier = {
					add = -20
					has_country_flag = GER_schleicher_cooperative_prussia
				}
				country_event = germany_spd_events.36 # Failure
			}
		}
	}
}

					has_game_rule = { rule = GER_path option = GER_PATH_SOCCON }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "KR_Event_Logging;GER Political Path - Schwander Cabinet"
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_spd_events.53 option germany_spd_events.53.a"
		name = germany_spd_events.53.a
		add_stability = -0.1
		hidden_effect = {
			GER_rudolf_schwander = { set_nationality = ROOT }
		}
		activate_advisor = GER_rudolf_schwander_sic
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_liberal
			election_frequency = 60
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			long_name = GER_schwander_party_long
			name = GER_schwander_party
		}
		set_country_flag = GER_schwander_government_happened
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_conservative }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_democrat }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		remove_mission = GER_coalition_relations
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GER_Government_Paralysis }
			}
			effect_tooltip = {
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = GER_paralysis_base
					add_idea = GER_paralysis_reduce_20
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { GER_government_paralysis_factor = 0.2 }
			clamp_variable = {
				var = GER_government_paralysis_factor
				max = 0
				min = -1
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { GER_government_paralysis_factor > -0.01 }
				}
				country_event = germany_spd_events.69
			}
		}
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
		hidden_effect = { country_event = germany_spd_events.64 }
	}
}

			}

					factor = 0

				}
				add_to_variable = {

					value = 5
					tooltip = GER_Z_loyalty_gain
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = GER_Z_loyalty max = 100 min = 0 }
			}
			20 = {

					factor = 0
					check_variable = { GER_Agrarian_loyalty < 1 }

				add_to_variable = {
					var = GER_Agrarian_loyalty
					value = 5

				}

	desc = germany_military_events.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_army

	is_triggered_only = yes

		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_military_events.1 option germany_military_events.1.a"
		name = germany_military_events.1.a
		set_country_flag = GER_military_mechanics_unlocked
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_military_mechanics_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					GER_is_du_path = yes
				}
				set_variable = { GER_military_faction_strength = 20 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					GER_is_swr_path = yes
				}
				set_variable = { GER_military_faction_strength = 50 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					GER_is_schleicher_path = yes
				}
				set_variable = { GER_military_faction_strength = 30 }
			}
			unlock_national_focus = GER_army_reform_stuff
		}
	}
}

		}

		add_war_support = -0.03
	}

	desc = germany_flavour_events.4.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_american_brigade

	is_triggered_only = yes

		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_flavour_events.4 option germany_flavour_events.4.a"
		name = germany_flavour_events.4.a
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = infantry_equipment
			amount = 1000
			producer = FROM
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		custom_override_tooltip = {
			tooltip = {
				localization_key = tooltip_create_division_template
				NAME = "Expeditions-Division Indochina"
				LINE_1 = { localization_key = line_battalion_tt NAME = infantry ICON = GFX_unit_infantry_icon_small COUNT = 6 }
				SUPPORT_1 = { localization_key = support_battalion_tt NAME = engineer ICON = GFX_unit_engineer_icon_small }
				SUPPORT_2 = { localization_key = support_battalion_tt NAME = recon ICON = GFX_unit_recon_icon_small }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_template = "Expeditions-Division Indochina" }
				delete_unit_template_and_units = { division_template = "Expeditions-Division Indochina" disband = yes } #no cheating
			}
			division_template = {
				name = "Expeditions-Division Indochina"
				division_names_group = GEA_INF_01
				regiments = {
					infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
					infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
					infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
					infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
					infantry = { x = 1 y = 2 }
				}
				support = {
					engineer = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					recon = { x = 0 y = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		capital_scope = {
			custom_override_tooltip = {
				tooltip = {
					localization_key = tooltip_spawn_unit
					TYPE = "Expeditions-Division Indochina"
				}
				create_unit = {
					division = "name = \"1. Expeditions-Division Indochina\" division_template = \"Expeditions-Division Indochina\" start_experience_factor = 0.8"
					owner = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
	}

country_event = { #hidden event to trigger Wilhelm's death even if GER is dead
	id = germany_flavour_events.8

	hidden = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = 64.owner #this needs to be a MTTH due to the variance in GER scenarios
		date > 1941.6.4
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_flavour_events.8 option 1"
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_leader = { character = GER_wilhelm_ii } }
			country_event = germany_flavour_events.9
			news_event = { id = germany_flavour_events.118 days = 1 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = MAF
				MAF = { has_country_leader = { character = GER_wilhelm_ii } }
			}
			MAF = {
				country_event = germany_flavour_events.9
				news_event = { id = germany_flavour_events.118 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		else = {
			GER_wilhelm_ii_dies = yes
		}
	}
}

	id = germany_flavour_events.25
	title = germany_flavour_events.25.t
	desc = germany_flavour_events.25.d

	trigger = {
		has_completed_focus = GER_von_schleicher_cabinet
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				long_name = GER_social_liberal_party_long
				name = GER_social_liberal_party
			}
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

				GER_is_du_path = yes

		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = GER_path option = GER_PATH_SOCDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = GER_path option = GER_PATH_SOCLIB }
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = GER_postwar_elections_held
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_conservative
			election_frequency = 60
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = GER_women_suffrage
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = GER_women_suffrage_event
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = GER_women_suffrage_event
			country_event = germany_flavour_events.108
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_completed_focus = GER_protect_states_rights }
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:authoritarian_democrat }
			add_to_coalition = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = GER_zentrum_left_chairman
			}
			activate_advisor = GER_carl_ulitzka_sic
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = GER_zentrum_compromise_board
			}
			activate_advisor = GER_konrad_adenauer_sic
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = GER_zentrum_centre_chairman
			}
			activate_advisor = GER_adam_stegerwald_sic
		}
		else = {
			activate_advisor = GER_fritz_schaffer_sic
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_flavour_events.25 option germany_flavour_events.25.b"
		name = germany_flavour_events.25.b
		trigger = {
			GER_is_du_path = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = GER_path option = GER_PATH_SOCCON }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = GER_women_suffrage
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = GER_women_suffrage_event
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = GER_women_suffrage_event
			country_event = germany_flavour_events.108
		}
		set_country_flag = GER_postwar_elections_held
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_democrat
			election_frequency = 60
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		activate_advisor = GER_theodor_haubach_sic
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_flavour_events.25 option germany_flavour_events.25.c1"

				limit = { is_in_coalition_with_paternal_autocrat = yes }
				set_country_flag = GER_has_pataut_coalition

				limit = { is_in_coalition_with_national_populist = yes }
				set_country_flag = GER_has_natpop_coalition
			}
			meta_effect = {
				text = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = var:current_party_ideology_group
						last_election = "[CURRENT_DATE]"
						election_frequency = 12

					}
				}
				CURRENT_DATE = "[?global.date.GetDateStringNoHour]"
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GER_has_soclib_coalition

					has_country_flag = GER_has_marklib_coalition

				add_to_coalition = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GER_has_soccon_coalition
				}
				set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_conservative }
				add_to_coalition = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GER_has_authdem_coalition
				}
				set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:authoritarian_democrat }
				add_to_coalition = yes

		}
		text = germany_flavour_events.41.d2
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_westarp

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_flavour_events.41 option germany_flavour_events.41.a"
		name = germany_flavour_events.41.a
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			GER_kuno_von_westarp = { set_nationality = ROOT }
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				long_name = GER_authoritarian_democrat_party_dnvu_long
				name = GER_authoritarian_democrat_party_dnvu
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
				long_name = GER_paternal_autocrat_party_dnvu_long2
				name = GER_paternal_autocrat_party_dnvu
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = GER_zentrum_swr_coalition
						has_country_flag = GER_federalist_union_established
					}
				}
				country_event = germany_flavour_events.102
			}
		}
		GER_ulrich_von_hassell = {
			remove_political_advisor_role = yes
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				long_name = GER_authoritarian_democrat_party_dnvu_long_fake
				name = GER_authoritarian_democrat_party_dnvu
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
				long_name = GER_paternal_autocrat_party_dnvu_long2_fake
				name = GER_paternal_autocrat_party_dnvu
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:paternal_autocrat }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = national_populist
			long_name = GER_national_populist_party_dnvu_long
			name = GER_national_populist_party_dnvu
		}
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:national_populist }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = GER_treviranus_co_chair
			}
			hidden_effect = { GER_gottfried_treviranus = { set_nationality = ROOT } }
			activate_advisor = GER_gottfried_treviranus_sic
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = GER_schlange_co_chair
			}
			GER_hans_schlange_schoningen = {
				hidden_effect = { set_nationality = ROOT }
				remove_political_advisor_role = yes
			}
			activate_advisor = GER_hans_schlange_schoningen_sic
		}
		else = { # just in case
			activate_advisor = GER_kuno_von_westarp_sic
		}
	}

	title = germany_flavour_events.55.t
	desc = germany_flavour_events.55.d

	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {

		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_flavour_events.55 option germany_flavour_events.55.a"
		name = germany_flavour_events.55.a
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		GER_kurt_von_schleicher = { retire = yes }
		hidden_effect = {
			GER_ferdinand_von_bredow = { set_nationality = ROOT }
			unlock_national_focus = GER_nationalise_prussian_secret_police
		}
		activate_advisor = GER_ferdinand_von_bredow_sic
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_flavour_events.55 option germany_flavour_events.55.b"
		name = germany_flavour_events.55.b
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = GER_tilmowsky_vice
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		GER_kurt_von_schleicher = { retire = yes }
		hidden_effect = {
			GER_tilo_wilmowsky = {
				set_nationality = ROOT
				remove_political_advisor_role = yes
			}
		}
		activate_advisor = GER_tilo_wilmowsky_sic
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_flavour_events.55 option germany_flavour_events.55.c"
		name = germany_flavour_events.55.c
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = GER_winnig_vice
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		GER_kurt_von_schleicher = { retire = yes }
		hidden_effect = {
			GER_august_winnig = {
				set_nationality = ROOT
			}
		}
		activate_advisor = GER_august_winnig_sic
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_flavour_events.55 option germany_flavour_events.55.e"
		name = germany_flavour_events.55.e
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		GER_kurt_von_schleicher = { retire = yes }
		activate_advisor = GER_carl_friedrich_goerdeler_sic
	}
	after = {
		# Turn you paternal_autocrat if you filled out the New State decisions.
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_idea = GER_new_state_6
					AND = {
						is_ai = yes
						has_game_rule = { rule = GER_path option = GER_PATH_SCHLEICHER_PATAUT }
					}
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = authoritarian_democrat
					popularity = -0.3
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = paternal_autocrat
					popularity = 0.3
				}
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:authoritarian_democrat }
			add_to_coalition = yes
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:national_populist }
			add_to_coalition = yes
			hidden_effect = {
				GER_increase_new_state_to_end = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = GER_red_general_absorb_aspd_flag
			}
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_democrat }
			add_to_coalition = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = GER_red_general_ally_national_liberals_flag
			}
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:market_liberal }
			add_to_coalition = yes
		}
	}
}

	desc = germany_flavour_events.67.d

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		has_cosmetic_tag = GER_rep
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_flavour_events.67 option germany_flavour_events.67.a"
		name = germany_flavour_events.67.a
		drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
		set_portraits = {
			character = GER_wilhelm_iv
			civilian = { large = GFX_portrait_GER_wilhelm_iv_civilian_large }
		}
		GER_wilhelm_iv = {
			set_character_name = GER_wilhelm_iv
			set_character_as_monarch = yes
		}
		GER_create_wilhelm_iv = yes
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = market_liberal
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = market_liberal
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_conservative }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:authoritarian_democrat }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GER_Republican_Constitution }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GER_Wilhelmine_Constitution }
		}
		add_advisor_role = {
			character = GER_karl_jarres
			advisor = {
				slot = political_advisor
				idea_token = GER_karl_jarres_advisor
				desc = GER_karl_jarres_leader_desc
				traits = { KR_steel_magnate }
				cost = 150
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_dvp_electable
	}

		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_flavour_events.67 option germany_flavour_events.67.b"

		add_stability = 0.05

			ideology = market_liberal
			popularity = -0.1
		}

				}
			}
		}
		if = {

			custom_effect_tooltip = GER_goering_resigns_tt
		}
	}

country_event = { # Women's suffrage?
	id = germany_flavour_events.93
	title = germany_flavour_events.93.t
	desc = germany_flavour_events.93.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_suffrags

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_flavour_events.93 option germany_flavour_events.93.a"
		name = germany_flavour_events.93.a
		ai_chance = { base = 25 }
		trigger = {
			GER_is_du_path = yes
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.01
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = GER_zentrum_right_chairman
			}
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = GER_Z_loyalty
				value = 20
				tooltip = GER_Z_loyalty_loss
			}
			clamp_variable = { var = GER_Z_loyalty min = 0 max = 100 }
		}
		else = {
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = GER_Z_loyalty
				value = 10
				tooltip = GER_Z_loyalty_loss
			}
			clamp_variable = { var = GER_Z_loyalty min = 0 max = 100 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GER_Z_loyalty < 1 }
				is_in_coalition_with_social_conservative = yes
			}
			activate_mission = GER_SPD_Z_rift
		}
		subtract_from_variable = {
			var = GER_Polish_loyalty
			value = 10
			tooltip = GER_Polish_loyalty_loss
		}
		clamp_variable = { var = GER_Polish_loyalty min = 0 max = 100 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GER_Polish_loyalty < 1 }
				has_country_flag = GER_poles_in_coalition
			}
			activate_mission = GER_SPD_Polish_rift
		}
		add_days_mission_timeout = {
			mission = GER_SPD_demand_action
			days = 30
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_flavour_events.93 option germany_flavour_events.93.b"
		name = germany_flavour_events.93.b
		ai_chance = { base = 25 }
		trigger = {
			GER_is_du_path = yes
		}
		add_political_power = 10
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = SPD_left_LVP_boosted
			}
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = GER_LVP_loyalty
				value = 15
				tooltip = GER_LVP_loyalty_loss
			}
			clamp_variable = { var = GER_LVP_loyalty min = 0 max = 100 }
		}
		else = {
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = GER_LVP_loyalty
				value = 10
				tooltip = GER_LVP_loyalty_loss
			}
		}
		clamp_variable = { var = GER_LVP_loyalty min = 0 max = 100 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GER_LVP_loyalty < 1 }
				is_in_coalition_with_social_liberal = yes
			}
			activate_mission = GER_SPD_LVP_rift
		}
		add_days_mission_timeout = {
			mission = GER_SPD_demand_action
			days = -30
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_flavour_events.93 option germany_flavour_events.93.c"
		name = germany_flavour_events.93.c
		ai_chance = { base = 25 }
		trigger = {
			GER_is_schleicher_path = yes
		}
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = THIS decision = GER_red_general_local_women_suffrage }
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = THIS decision = GER_red_general_reichsfrauenbund }
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_flavour_events.93 option germany_flavour_events.93.e"
		name = germany_flavour_events.93.e
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = GER_schleicher_ai
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			GER_is_du_path = no
		}
		add_stability = -0.02
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = 0.01
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Another epic Schacht banger
	id = germany_flavour_events.113
	title = germany_flavour_events.113.t
	desc = germany_flavour_events.113.d

	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = FRA
			has_country_flag = GER_schacht_removed
			is_ai = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_flavour_events.113 option germany_flavour_events.113.a"
		name = germany_flavour_events.113.a
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_cuts_debt_tt
		add_political_power = 25
		add_stability = -0.06
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = GER_austerity_program
			days = 365
		}
		add_to_variable = { GER_debt = -7 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = GER_red_general
				GER_kurt_von_schleicher = { is_second_in_command = yes }
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = GER_schleicher_move_right
			add_to_variable = { GER_schleicher_ideology = -20 }
			clamp_variable = { var = GER_schleicher_ideology max = 100 min = 0 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_active_mission = GER_SPD_demand_action
			}
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = GER_SPD_demand_action
				days = -45
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				GER_is_du_path = yes
			}
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = GER_Left_SPD_loyalty
				value = 20
				tooltip = GER_Left_SPD_loyalty_loss
			}
			clamp_variable = { var = GER_Left_SPD_loyalty min = 0 max = 100 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { GER_Left_SPD_loyalty < 1 }
					has_country_flag = GER_left_spd_in_coalition
				}
				activate_mission = GER_SPD_Left_rift
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				GER_is_swr_path = yes
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = GER_effect_increases_dkp_tt
			add_to_variable = { GER_swr_coalition_balance = -15 }
			GER_check_swr_coalition_strength = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = germany_flavour_events.113 days = 365 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_flavour_events.113 option germany_flavour_events.113.b"
		name = germany_flavour_events.113.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				AND = {
					GER_is_swr_path = yes
					has_character = GER_hjalmar_schacht
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = social_democrat
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GER_Government_Paralysis }
				}
				effect_tooltip = {
					swap_ideas = {
						remove_idea = GER_paralysis_reduce_5
						add_idea = GER_paralysis_base
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = { GER_government_paralysis_factor = -0.05 }
				clamp_variable = {
					var = GER_government_paralysis_factor
					max = 0
					min = -1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = social_democrat
					if = {
						limit = { is_ai = no }
						check_variable = { GER_government_paralysis_factor < -0.49 }
					}
					else = {
						check_variable = { GER_government_paralysis_factor < -0.69 }
					}
				}
				country_event = germany_spd_events.53
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = GER_zentrum_left_chairman
					}
				}
				subtract_from_variable = {
					var = GER_Z_loyalty
					value = 10
					tooltip = GER_Z_loyalty_loss
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = GER_Z_loyalty min = 0 max = 100 }
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { GER_Z_loyalty < 1 }
						is_in_coalition_with_social_conservative = yes
					}
					activate_mission = GER_SPD_Z_rift
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_in_coalition_with_social_liberal = yes }
				subtract_from_variable = {
					var = GER_LVP_loyalty
					value = 15
					tooltip = GER_LVP_loyalty_loss
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = GER_LVP_loyalty min = 0 max = 100 }
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { GER_LVP_loyalty < 1 }
					}
					activate_mission = GER_SPD_LVP_rift
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_political_power = -75
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GER_zentrum_swr_coalition
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
				custom_effect_tooltip = GER_zentrum_swr_coalition_hurts_tt
				add_to_variable = { GER_Zentrum_seats_r = -3 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character = GER_hjalmar_schacht }
			custom_effect_tooltip = {
				localization_key = tooltip_disable_political_advisor
				ADVISOR = GER_hjalmar_schacht
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				retire_character = GER_hjalmar_schacht
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = GER_unlocked_schacht_decision
				}
			}
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = THIS decision = GER_remove_schacht }
			set_country_flag = GER_unlocked_schacht_decision
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = germany_flavour_events.113 days = 365 }
		}
	}
	option = { #cheap first round for SWR
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_flavour_events.113 option germany_flavour_events.113.c"
		name = germany_flavour_events.113.c
		trigger = {
			GER_is_swr_path = yes
			has_character = GER_hjalmar_schacht
		}
		add_political_power = -30
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = GER_zentrum_swr_coalition
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			custom_effect_tooltip = GER_zentrum_swr_coalition_hurts_tt
			add_to_variable = { GER_Zentrum_seats_r = -1 }
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = market_liberal
			popularity = 0.01
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = {
			localization_key = tooltip_disable_political_advisor
			ADVISOR = GER_hjalmar_schacht
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			retire_character = GER_hjalmar_schacht
		}
	}

# egg
country_event = { #egg basket
	id = germany_easter_egg_events.0

	hidden = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		original_tag = GER
		surrender_progress > 0.5
		is_in_faction = yes
		has_war_with = FRA
		has_war_with = RUS
		num_divisions < var:FRA.num_divisions # FRA has more divisions than GER
		num_divisions < var:RUS.num_divisions # RUS has more divisions than GER
		any_owned_state = { # GER still controls at least one coastal state, so the Kaiser can escape.
			is_in_home_area = yes
			is_coastal = yes
			is_controlled_by_ROOT_or_ally = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_easter_egg_events.0 option 1"
		if = {
			limit = { GER_is_schleicher_path = yes }
			country_event = { id = germany_easter_egg_events.1 days = 5 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_government = social_democrat }
			country_event = { id = germany_easter_egg_events.3 days = 5 }
		}
		#space for S-W-R eggs goes here
	}
}
country_event = { # egg
	id = germany_easter_egg_events.1
	title = germany_easter_egg_events.1.t
	desc = germany_easter_egg_events.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_march

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		GER_is_schleicher_path = yes
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_easter_egg_events.1 option germany_easter_egg_events.1.a"
		name = germany_easter_egg_events.1.a
		add_political_power = -100
		add_stability = -0.10
		add_manpower = -500
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = germany_easter_egg_events.2 days = 10 }
		}
	}
}
country_event = { # egg
	id = germany_easter_egg_events.2
	title = germany_easter_egg_events.2.t
	desc = germany_easter_egg_events.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_march

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_easter_egg_events.2 option germany_easter_egg_events.2.a"
		name = germany_easter_egg_events.2.a
		add_war_support = 0.1
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = national_populist
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
				long_name = GER_bauer_front_party_long
				name = GER_bauer_front_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = national_populist
				long_name = GER_bauer_front_party_long
				name = GER_bauer_front_party
			}
			GER_waldemar_pabst = { set_nationality = ROOT }
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					GER_is_in_mitteleuropa = yes
				}
				GER_remove_from_mitteleuropa = yes
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:national_populist }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		add_country_leader_role = {
			character = GER_max_bauer
			country_leader = {
				desc = GER_max_bauer_leader_desc
				ideology = paternal_autocrat_subtype
			}
			promote_leader = yes
		}
		add_country_leader_role = {
			character = GER_max_bauer
			country_leader = {
				desc = GER_max_bauer_leader_desc
				ideology = national_populist_subtype
			}
			promote_leader = yes
		}
		activate_advisor = GER_waldemar_pabst_sic
		hidden_effect = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = GER_war
			set_country_flag = GER_bauer_putsch
			GER_wilhelm_iii = { clr_character_flag = show_unit_leader_role } #TODO: revert when bug with country_leader variable is fixed
			GER_rupprecht_von_bayern = { clr_character_flag = show_unit_leader_role } #TODO: revert when bug with country_leader variable is fixed
		}
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
		unlock_national_focus = GER_bauer_putsch
	}
}

country_event = { # egg
	id = germany_easter_egg_events.4
	title = germany_easter_egg_events.4.t
	desc = germany_easter_egg_events.4.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_march

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germany_easter_egg_events.4 option germany_easter_egg_events.4.a"
		name = germany_easter_egg_events.4.a
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		GER_hermann_muller = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_ideology = social_democrat_subtype }
				promote_character = social_democrat_subtype
			}
			else = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					country_leader = {
						desc = GER_hermann_muller_sic_desc
						ideology = social_democrat_subtype
					}
					promote_leader = yes
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			GER_hofgeismar_circle = { retire = yes }
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = GER_SPD_rebellion }
				remove_ideas = GER_SPD_rebellion
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character = GER_wilhelm_ii }
				GER_wilhelm_ii = { retire = yes }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character = GER_wilhelm_iii }
				GER_wilhelm_iii = {
					retire = yes
					clr_character_flag = show_unit_leader_role #TODO: revert when bug with country_leader variable is fixed
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character = GER_rupprecht_von_bayern }
				GER_rupprecht_von_bayern = {
					retire = yes
					clr_character_flag = show_unit_leader_role #TODO: revert when bug with country_leader variable is fixed
				}
			}
			GER_theodor_haubach = { set_nationality = ROOT }
		}
		activate_advisor = GER_theodor_haubach_sic
		set_cosmetic_tag = GER_rep
		set_country_flag = GER_republic_established
		unlock_national_focus = GER_the_republic
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
	}
}
